      - $(SYMBOL).fIlluminatorPercent

        | io: output

      - waveform
      - Descriptive name for the LED
      - | autosave_pass0: VAL DESC
        | io: output


    * - $(PREFIX):NAME_RBV
      - waveform

      - | autosave_pass0: VAL DESC
        | io: output


    * - $(PREFIX):PWR
      - bo

      - | field: ONAM ON
        | field: ZNAM OFF
        | io: output


    * - $(PREFIX):PWR_RBV
      - bi

      - | field: ONAM ON
        | field: ZNAM OFF
        | io: output
